		<aside id="text-2" class="widget inner-padding widget_text"><h2 class="widget-title">About Me</h2>			<div class="textwidget"><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><center></center><img loading="eager" decoding="async" class="wp-image-2850 size-thumbnail aligncenter" src="https://notimerecipe.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/05/Meghan-author-150x150.webp" alt="Meghan" width="150" height="150" data-wp-editing="1" srcset="https://www.notimerecipe.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/05/Meghan-author-150x150.webp 150w, https://www.notimerecipe.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/05/Meghan-author-180x180.webp 180w, https://www.notimerecipe.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/05/Meghan-author.webp 200w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px"  fetchpriority="high"/></p>
<p data-start="77" data-end="218">At NotimeRecipe, we understand how overwhelming it can feel to get dinner on the table when life gets busy.</p>
<p data-start="77" data-end="218">Between work, errands, and all the little things that pile up, spending hours in the kitchen just isn’t always feasible. But that doesn’t mean you have to settle for bland, uninspiring meals.</p>
<p data-start="77" data-end="218">We believe great food should be accessible to everyone, even on the busiest days.</p>
<div style="border: 2px solid #e292a8; padding: 15px; margin: 10px; background-color: #ffffff00; text-align: center;"><a style="color: #575760; font-weight: 600; font-size: 18px; text-decoration: none; transition: color 0.3s ease;" href="https://notimerecipe.com/about-us/">Recipe of Our Life</a></div>
</div>
